msg:This hot spring hotel has different changes and beauty throughout the year. 3 days and 2 nights is not enough to play, but it is still very good.

First of all: check-in is at the foot of the mountain, the space is large, and the service is very nice. There will be a vehicle to take you to the room on the mountain.

Secondly, the villa is a private hot spring, and you can arrange a waiter to help you open the hot spring water and soak in the hot spring ‚ô®Ô∏è. The upper part is the living room, and the lower part is the room. The area is very large. It is recommended to stay in two rooms for up to 5 people (3 adults and 2 children) or 4 adults, because one room has a bed of 1.8 meters and the other room has a large bed. The living room has a kitchen and a refrigerator, which is suitable for home parties and the space is large enough. Every room has a beautiful view.

Then, the breakfast is rich in quality, and there are also wontons that Shanghai people like to eat. It is still very pleasant to taste breakfast on the terrace in this weather. Because in the mountains, the air is good and surrounded by nature. The Indian waiter üíÅ‚ôÇÔ∏è is gentle and polite.

It is worth mentioning that the hydrangeas are beautifully photographed, and they are all in full bloom on the mountain. I really want to pick one, hahaha. There are also fireflies in this season, you can let your children learn about and appreciate them, but remember not to catch them, they seem to be second-level protected animals.

Finally: Shenma Farm (you can go there with your room card) ponies, take a stroll, feed the small animals.

The scenery on the hillside, the wildness of hydrangeas, the company of fireflies, the ponies at Shenma Ranch, a relaxing weekend that you will never get tired of.

name:S‚Äçh‚Äçe‚Äçn‚Äçn‚Äçi‚Äçk‚Äçe
info:Featured Room - 1-Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Couples
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 9, 2024
msg:First of all, thank you to the housekeeper Zhang Mingli. She added WeChat before departure and actively contacted her to prepare for our arrival in advance.

The one-bedroom was great, with large floor-to-ceiling windows and a big pine tree next to the terrace. Although it only had a mountain view, the relaxation and joy in the mountains and fields was so healing that when I got to the room, I put down my luggage and didn‚Äôt even have time to pack it up. I just stayed there. Sitting on the sofa in front of the bed, I watched various tits chirping in the forest. The only regret is that the squirrels are all hibernating now.

Because it is a one-bedroom apar**ent, there is no outdoor pool. An indoor bathtub is provided. The hot spring water is very light blue-green. The disposable toiletries provided are from L'Occitane. The hotel is very thoughtful and also prepares disposable toiletries. The bathtub cover and even the toilet are equipped with disposable seat covers. The toilet is a Washlet and comes with a footrest for children, which is really parent-child friendly.

There will be fruits every day when you stay. Strawberries on the first day and tangerines on the second day. The quality of the fruits is great, fresh and sweet.
The charged snacks and drinks at the bar are reasonably priced. A can of Coke costs ¬•10, which is almost the same price as in a hotel. After all, in hotels, there is almost no takeout available.

In fact, the temperature in the mountains is relatively low. We went to the city to have dinner. Before departure, the temperature was +5.5 degrees. When we returned to the hotel, the temperature had dropped to -0.5 degrees. However, the room was not cold at all because there was floor heating. There is also air conditioning, double buffs are fully stacked, and you won‚Äôt feel cold even if you wear short-sleeved clothes in the room. Compared with last month, Kasuke Hoshino, who lives in Tiantai Mountain, made me shiver at room temperature. People who are afraid of the cold really have it here. Moved.

Breakfast is not rich, but the basic configuration is there. In fact, no matter where it is, there are only a few choices for buffet breakfast. If you like Western-style food, there are sausages, fried eggs, toast slices, cereals, milk, and yogurt. Chinese dishes include fried noodles, fried rice, steamed grains, porridge, side dishes, etc. Traditional Chinese breakfast also includes fried dough sticks, sesame balls, soy milk, and steamed buns. There are also freshly cooked noodles and chicken soup wontons.
Especially cue the steamed waxy corn, it‚Äôs especially delicious! Very soft and waxy, with a hint of sweetness. I ate corn for breakfast for two days in a row. . . .
In addition, I would like to mention that the real feature of the breakfast is that most of the vegetables are grown at the Shenma Farm next door, focusing on freshness and originality.

In the summer, at the end of June and the beginning of July, you can still see fireflies. The fireflies must be extremely polluting to the environment, otherwise the fireflies will disappear. But it is estimated that housing prices will be very high by then. Who can refuse to watch fireflies in the mountains? ~~~There will definitely be a lot of naughty and domineering little squirrels there by then. In addition, the housekeeper said that the open-air infinity pool is also very impressive.

The hotel also has a trail around the mountain, which is about 5 kilometers in total. The scenery is very good, and the trail is also very clean. There are dead branches and fallen leaves, but no garbage. It is very popular. From time to time, there are small tits chasing and flying around. , and there are stretches of bamboo forest. You can also take a breath of fresh air during the 0-difficulty hiking.

For a three-day and two-night trip, we recommend:
Arrive at noon on the first day and take the mountain trail in the afternoon.
In the evening, after dining at a nearby farmhouse, come back and take a bath.

The next day you can go to Nanshan Bamboo Sea in the morning and Tianmu Lake in the afternoon.
In the evening, go to the city to have dinner and come back to take a bath.

On the third day, after breakfast, we checked out and drove to Yixing Dajue Temple.
After shopping, we headed straight home.
